    `FlightNo` varchar(5) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 NOT NULL,
    `Capacity` int NOT NULL,
    `Current_Pass` int NOT NULL,
    `Origin` varchar(3) CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 NOT NULL,
